4504WSNCKN3353Y	1312210386557	007647010	HYDROCHLORIC ACID (1995 AND AFTER "ACID AEROSOLS" ONLY)	TRI	2012	SUNCOKE ENERGY MIDDLETOWN OPERATIONS	3353 YANKEE RD	MIDDLETOWN	BUTLER	OH	45044	YES	NO	NO	NO								324199						39.515058	-84.398276									SUNCOKE ENERGY	617339031	SunCoke Energy Middletown Operations (MTO) is a new facility that commenced operation in late October 2011.  As a result, its 2011 TRI report only included information from MTO's first 2 months of operation while the plant was still in start-up mode and not at its full coke production capacity.  MTO did not startup its pollution control system for treating the Hydrochloric Acid emissions generated by the plant's coke ovens until December 2011, and as a result its 2011 and 2012 Hydrochloric Acid release data is not linear with the plant's coal usage and coke production amounts.In addition, MTO utilized a revised emission factor to calculate the Hydrochloric Acid emissions manufactured and released amounts for the 2012 TRI report.  The new emission factor (which was determined via stack testing data from MTO's April & June 2012 compliance tests) is approximately 95% lower than the previous emission factor which was used for the 2011 TRI report (i.e. the previous factor was based on the allowable Hydrochloric Acid emissions limit in MTO's air permit).  Consequently, MTO's 2012 TRI report shows a significant reduction in the production normalized manufactured, treated, and released amounts for Hydrochloric Acid.|PRAI:Ratio is calculated from annual coal usage (wet tons).|NPYF:2011 TRI report was submitted via paper.
